## Outgrow privacy policy - Data Deletion Policy
- file: data/exec-logs/research-sprint/2026-03-13_151235_outgrow_privacy_policy.html
- pattern: Data Deletion Policy
- match_line: 2090
    			<h4 class="Privacy-subheading">Responsibility of visitors</h4>
    			<p>
    				Outgrow has not reviewed, and cannot review, all of the material posted to the Site or any third party site that the Site links to, and cannot therefore be responsible for that material’s content, use or effects. By operating the Site, Outgrow does not represent or imply that it endorses the material there posted, or that it believes such material to be accurate, useful or non-harmful. You are responsible for taking precautions as necessary to protect yourself and your computer systems from viruses, worms, Trojan horses, and other harmful or destructive content. The Site may contain content that is offensive, indecent, or otherwise objectionable, as well as content containing technical inaccuracies, typographical mistakes, and other errors. The Site may also contain material that violates the privacy or publicity rights, or infringes the intellectual property and other proprietary rights, of third parties, or the downloading, copying or use of which is subject to additional terms and conditions, stated or unstated. Outgrow disclaims any responsibility for any harm resulting from the use by visitors of the Site, or from any downloading by those visitors of content there posted.
    			</p>
    			<h4 class="Privacy-subheading">Data Deletion Policy</h4>
    			<h5>1. Individual Rights</h5>
    			<p>An individual has the right to erasure, also known as ‘the right to be forgotten’. The principle underpinning this right is to enable an individual to request the deletion or removal of personal data where there is no compelling reason for its continued processing.</p>
    			<h5>2. When does the right to erasure apply?</h5>
    			<p>Individuals have a right to have personal data erased and to prevent processing in specific circumstances:</p>
    			<ul >
    				<li class="li-style">Where the personal data is no longer necessary in relation to the purpose for which it was originally collected/processed;</li>
    				<li class="li-style">When the individual withdraws consent;</li>
    				<li class="li-style">When the individual objects to the processing and there is no other legal ground for the relevant
     processing activity;</li>
     <li class="li-style">When the personal data was unlawfully processed;</li>
     <li class="li-style">Where the personal data has to be erased in order to comply with a legal obligation.</li>
    			</ul>
    			<h5>3. How can data be deleted?</h5>
    			<p>
    			You can delete any of your outgrow user data at any time, by going to <a href="https://outgrow.co/">outgrow.co</a>, logging into your account and then clicking user details, and there you can choose which user you would like to delete and on the right side of each user row there is a delete option. This will allow you to delete the user data directly from your account. You can also reach out to us at <a href="mailto:questions@outgrow.co">questions@outgrow.co</a> to help with any data deletion request. You can also delete the content you build on Outgrow by going to your dashboard and selecting the content you want deleted and on the top right you can select the content and delete it. Note: Only do this if you are 100% sure you want your content deleted as Outgrow will not be able to retrieve it once its permanently deleted.
    			</p>
    			<p>Some data may still remain in the systems back-up files, which will be deleted periodically.</p>
    			<p>If you reach out to us for a data deletion request, we undertake to perform the deletion within 15 business days and will send you a confirmation once the information has been deleted. Wherever possible, we will aim to complete the request in advance of the deadline. </p>
    		
    		      
    			<h4 class="Privacy-subheading">Use of Workspace APIs and User Data</h4>
    			 <p> <a href = "https://outgrow.co">Outgrow.co </a> uses Workspace APIs to enhance our services and provide a personalized experience for our users. We want to clarify how we handle the data obtained through these APIs: </p>
                <h5>1. Data Retention </h5> <p> We do not retain user data obtained through Workspace APIs for the purpose of developing, improving, or training generalized AI and/or ML models.</p>
                <h5>2. Data Usage </h5> <p>The data collected through Workspace APIs is used solely to improve our service delivery, enhance user experience, and support specific user interactions as detailed in our service agreements.</p>
    				<h5>3. Data Protection </h5> <p>We employ industry-standard security measures to protect user data obtained through Workspace APIs and ensure it is used in compliance with applicable laws and regulations.</p>
    				<h5>4. User Rights </h5> <p>Users have the right to inquire about the data collected through Workspace APIs and request its deletion. </p>
    			
    				<h4 class="Privacy-subheading">Privacy</h4>
    			<p>
    			You consent to the transfer, storage, and processing of your information – including the content you posted or transferred to the site and any personal information – to and within the European Union.

## Outgrow privacy policy - backups may retain data
- file: data/exec-logs/research-sprint/2026-03-13_151235_outgrow_privacy_policy.html
- pattern: back-?up
- match_line: 2107
    			<h5>3. How can data be deleted?</h5>
    			<p>
    			You can delete any of your outgrow user data at any time, by going to <a href="https://outgrow.co/">outgrow.co</a>, logging into your account and then clicking user details, and there you can choose which user you would like to delete and on the right side of each user row there is a delete option. This will allow you to delete the user data directly from your account. You can also reach out to us at <a href="mailto:questions@outgrow.co">questions@outgrow.co</a> to help with any data deletion request. You can also delete the content you build on Outgrow by going to your dashboard and selecting the content you want deleted and on the top right you can select the content and delete it. Note: Only do this if you are 100% sure you want your content deleted as Outgrow will not be able to retrieve it once its permanently deleted.
    			</p>
    			<p>Some data may still remain in the systems back-up files, which will be deleted periodically.</p>
    			<p>If you reach out to us for a data deletion request, we undertake to perform the deletion within 15 business days and will send you a confirmation once the information has been deleted. Wherever possible, we will aim to complete the request in advance of the deadline. </p>
    		
    		      
    			<h4 class="Privacy-subheading">Use of Workspace APIs and User Data</h4>
    			 <p> <a href = "https://outgrow.co">Outgrow.co </a> uses Workspace APIs to enhance our services and provide a personalized experience for our users. We want to clarify how we handle the data obtained through these APIs: </p>
                <h5>1. Data Retention </h5> <p> We do not retain user data obtained through Workspace APIs for the purpose of developing, improving, or training generalized AI and/or ML models.</p>
                <h5>2. Data Usage </h5> <p>The data collected through Workspace APIs is used solely to improve our service delivery, enhance user experience, and support specific user interactions as detailed in our service agreements.</p>
    				<h5>3. Data Protection </h5> <p>We employ industry-standard security measures to protect user data obtained through Workspace APIs and ensure it is used in compliance with applicable laws and regulations.</p>
    				<h5>4. User Rights </h5> <p>Users have the right to inquire about the data collected through Workspace APIs and request its deletion. </p>
    			
    				<h4 class="Privacy-subheading">Privacy</h4>
    			<p>
    			You consent to the transfer, storage, and processing of your information – including the content you posted or transferred to the site and any personal information – to and within the European Union.
    			<h5>
    				Gathering of Personally-Identifying Information
    			</h5>
    			<p>
    				Certain visitors to Outgrow’s websites choose to interact with Outgrow in ways that require Outgrow to gather personally-identifying information. The amount and type of information that Outgrow gathers depends on the nature of the interaction. In each case, Outgrow collects such information only as is necessary or appropriate to fulfill the purpose of the visitor’s interaction with Outgrow. Outgrow does not disclose personally-identifying information other than as described below. And visitors can always refuse to supply personally-identifying information, with the caveat that it may prevent them from engaging in certain website-related activities.
    			</p>
    			<h5>Aggregated Statistics</h5>

## ConvertCalculator privacy - Security section
- file: data/exec-logs/research-sprint/2026-03-13_150928_convert_privacy.html

                </style><div class="framer-1t0jkii" style="transform:none" data-framer-component-type="RichTextContainer"><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">Your privacy is critically important to us. At ConvertCalculator, we have a few fundamental principles:</p><ul class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7"><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">We are thoughtful about the personal information we ask you to provide and the personal information that we collect about you through the operation of our services.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">We store personal information for only as long as we have a reason to keep it.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">We aim to make it as simple as possible for you to control what information on your website is shared publicly (or kept private), indexed by search engines, and permanently deleted.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">We help protect you from overreaching government demands for your personal information.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">We aim for full transparency on how we gather, use, and share your personal information.</p></li></ul><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">Below is our Privacy Policy, which incorporates and clarifies these principles.</p><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">Who We Are and What This Policy Covers</h2><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">Hi there! We are the guys behind ConvertCalculator.com, a embeddable web calculator that let's your create calculators (e.g. price quote calculators) to be embedded on your website.</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">This Privacy Policy applies to information that we collect about you when you use app.convertcalculator.co and when your website visitors interact with an embeddable widget.</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">Throughout this Privacy Policy we’ll refer to our website, mobile applications and other products and services collectively as “Services.”</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">Please note that this Privacy Policy does not apply to any of our products or services that have a separate privacy policy.</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">Below we explain how we collect, use, and share information about you, along with the choices that you have with respect to that information.</p><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">Information We Collect</h2><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">We only collect information about you if we have a reason to do so–for example, to provide our Services, to communicate with you, or to make our Services better.</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">We collect information in three ways: if and when you provide information to us, automatically through operating our Services, and from outside sources. Let’s go over the information that we collect.</p><h3 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-i3b3hg" data-styles-preset="Btq2R0K0E">Information You Provide to Us</h3><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">It’s probably no surprise that we collect information that you provide to us. The amount and type of information depends on the context and how we use the information. Here are some examples:</p><ul class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7"><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Basic Account Information:</strong>&nbsp;We ask for basic information from you in order to set up your account. For example, we require individuals who sign up for a app.convertcalculator.co account to provide a name, email address, password and that’s it. You may set other information like Company name, but this is not required.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Transaction and Billing Information:</strong>&nbsp;If you buy something from us, you will provide additional personal and payment information that is required to process the transaction and your payment, such as your credit card information, and contact information.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Content Information:</strong>&nbsp;Depending on the Services you use, you may also provide us with information about you. For example, if you add information about you or your company in a calculator, we will have this information, and so will anyone with access to the Internet if you choose to embed the calculator on a public page on your website.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Communications With Us (Hi There!):</strong>&nbsp;You may also provide us information when you respond to surveys, communicate with support, or any other way you contact us by posting (in the future maybe public forums).</p></li></ul><h3 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-i3b3hg" data-styles-preset="Btq2R0K0E">Information We Collect Automatically</h3><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">We also collect some information automatically:</p><ul class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7"><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Log Information:</strong>&nbsp;Like most online service providers, we collect information that web browsers, mobile devices, and servers typically make available, such as the browser type, IP address, unique device identifiers, language preference, referring site, the date and time of access, operating system, and mobile network information. We collect log information when you use our Services.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Usage Information:</strong>&nbsp;We collect information about your usage of our Services. For example, we collection event data, along with information about your device (e.g., screen size, name of cellular network, and mobile device manufacturer). We also collect information (such as referring domain) when an embedded calculator get loaded (your website visitor interacts with it). We use this information to, for example, provide our Services to you, as well as get insights on how people use our Services, so we can make our Services better.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Location Information:</strong>&nbsp;We may determine the approximate location of your device from your IP address. We collect and use this information to, for example, calculate how many people visit our Services from certain geographic regions.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Information from Cookies &amp; Other Technologies:</strong>&nbsp;A cookie is a string of information that a website stores on a visitor’s computer, and that the visitor’s browser provides to the website each time the visitor returns. Pixel tags (also called web beacons) are small blocks of code placed on websites and emails. ConvertCalculator uses cookies and other technologies like pixel tags to help us identify and track visitors, usage, and access preferences for our Services, as well as track and understand email campaign effectiveness and to deliver targeted ads. For more information about our use of cookies and other technologies for tracking, including how you can control the use of cookies, please see our Cookie Policy.</p></li></ul><h3 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-i3b3hg" data-styles-preset="Btq2R0K0E">Information We Collect from Other Sources</h3><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">We may also get information about you from other sources. For example, if you connect with a external service (such as Stripe), we will receive information from that service (such as your username, basic profile information, and friends list) via the authorization procedures used by that service. The information we receive depends on which services you authorize and any options that are available.</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">We may also get information, such as a mailing address, from third party services about individuals who are not yet our users (…but we hope will be!), which we may use, for example, for marketing and advertising purposes like postcards and other mailers advertising our services.</p><h3 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-i3b3hg" data-styles-preset="Btq2R0K0E">Information we collect from the Google Sheets integration</h3><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">When authorizing us to use your Google user data, we collect spreadsheet properties when you integrate a calculator with Google Sheets. We access a list of your Google Drive files in order for you to pick a spreadsheet. When you selected a spreadsheet, we access the spreadsheet's properties to present you the option to choose the preferred worksheet. After that, we read the first row's values in order for you to connect calculator form fields to spreadsheet columns. When a submission is made on your calculator, we append the calculator form field values to the selected spreadsheet. In terms of storage, we only save the Spreadsheet ID and the sheet ID (also called Worksheet ID). We don't share any Google user data.</p><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">How And Why We Use Information</h2><h3 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-i3b3hg" data-styles-preset="Btq2R0K0E">Purposes for Using Information</h3><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">We use information about you as mentioned above and for the purposes listed below:</p><ul class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7"><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">To provide our Services–for example, to set up and maintain your account, host your embed code, or charge you for any of our paid Services;</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">To further develop and improve our Services–for example by adding new features that we think our users will enjoy or will help them to create and manage their websites more efficiently;</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">To monitor and analyze trends and better understand how users interact with our Services, which helps us improve our Services and make them easier to use;</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">To measure, gauge, and improve the effectiveness of our advertising, and better understand user retention and attrition–for example, we may analyze how many individuals purchased a plan after receiving a marketing message or the features used by those who continue to use our Services after a certain length of time;</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">To monitor and prevent any problems with our Services, protect the security of our Services, detect and prevent fraudulent transactions and other illegal activities, fight spam, and protect the rights and property of ConvertCalculator and others, which may result in us declining a transaction or the use of our Services;</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">To communicate with you, for example through an email, about offers and promotions offered by ConvertCalculator and others we think will be of interest to you, solicit your feedback, or keep you up to date on ConvertCalculator and our products; and</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">To personalize your experience using our Services, target our marketing messages to groups of our users (for example, those who have a particular plan with us or have been our user for a certain length of time), and serve relevant advertisements.</p></li></ul><h3 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-i3b3hg" data-styles-preset="Btq2R0K0E">Legal Bases for Collecting and Using Information</h3><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">A note here for those in the European Union about our legal grounds for processing information about you under EU data protection laws, which is that our use of your information is based on the grounds that:</p><ol class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7"><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">The use is necessary in order to fulfill our commitments to you under our Terms of Service or other agreements with you or is necessary to administer your account–for example, in order to enable access to our website on your device or charge you for a paid plan; or</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">The use is necessary for compliance with a legal obligation; or</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">The use is necessary in order to protect your vital interests or those of another person; or</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">We have a legitimate interest in using your information–for example, to provide and update our Services, to improve our Services so that we can offer you an even better user experience, to safeguard our Services, to communicate with you, to measure, gauge, and improve the effectiveness of our advertising, and better understand user retention and attrition, to monitor and prevent any problems with our Services, and to personalize your experience; or</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">You have given us your consent–for example when you create your account.</p></li></ol><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">Sharing Information</h2><h3 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-i3b3hg" data-styles-preset="Btq2R0K0E">How We Share Information</h3><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">We do not sell our users’ private personal information.</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">We share information about you in the limited circumstances spelled out below and with appropriate safeguards on your privacy:</p><ul class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7"><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Subsidiaries, Employees, and Independent Contractors:</strong>&nbsp;We may disclose information about you to our subsidiaries, our employees, and individuals who are our independent contractors that need to know the information in order to help us provide our Services or to process the information on our behalf. We require our subsidiaries, employees, and independent contractors to follow this Privacy Policy for personal information that we share with them.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Third Party Vendors:</strong>&nbsp;We may share information about you with third party vendors who need to know information about you in order to provide their services to us, or to provide their services to you or your site. This group includes vendors that help us provide our Services to you (like payment providers that process your credit and debit card information, fraud prevention services that allow us to analyze fraudulent payment transactions, postal and email delivery services that help us stay in touch with you, customer chat and email support services that help us communicate with you, those that assist us with our marketing efforts (e.g. by providing tools for identifying a specific marketing target group or improving our marketing campaigns), those that help us understand and enhance our Services (like analytics providers). We require vendors to agree to privacy commitments in order to share information with them.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Legal Requests:</strong>&nbsp;We may disclose information about you in response to a subpoena, court order, or other governmental request.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">To Protect Rights, Property, and Others:</strong>&nbsp;We may disclose information about you when we believe in good faith that disclosure is reasonably necessary to protect the property or rights of ConvertCalculator, third parties, or the public at large. For example, if we have a good faith belief that there is an imminent danger of death or serious physical injury, we may disclose information related to the emergency without delay.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Business Transfers:</strong>&nbsp;In connection with any merger, sale of company assets, or acquisition of all or a portion of our business by another company, or in the unlikely event that ConvertCalculator goes out of business or enters bankruptcy, user information would likely be one of the assets that is transferred or acquired by a third party. If any of these events were to happen, this Privacy Policy would continue to apply to your information and the party receiving your information may continue to use your information, but only consistent with this Privacy Policy.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">With Your Consent:</strong>&nbsp;We may share and disclose information with your consent or at your direction. For example, we may share your information with third parties with which you authorize us to do so, such as the social media services that you connect to your site through our Publicize feature.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Aggregated or De-Identified Information:</strong>&nbsp;We may share information that has been aggregated or reasonably de-identified, so that the information could not reasonably be used to identify you. For instance, we may publish aggregate statistics about the use of our Services and we may share a hashed version of your email address to facilitate customized ad campaigns on other platforms.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Published Support Requests:</strong>&nbsp;And if you send us a request (for example, via a support email or one of our feedback mechanisms), we reserve the right to publish that request in order to help us clarify or respond to your request or to help us support other users.</p></li></ul><h3 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-i3b3hg" data-styles-preset="Btq2R0K0E">Information Shared Publicly</h3><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">Information that you choose to make public is–you guessed it–disclosed publicly.</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">That means, of course, that all information you put in a calculator that you embed on your website, are all available to others–and we hope you get a lot of visitors!</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">Public information may also be indexed by search engines or used by third parties.</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">Please keep all of this in mind when deciding what you would like to share.</p><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">How Long We Keep Information</h2><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">We generally discard information about you when we no longer need the information for the purposes for which we collect and use it–which are described in the section above on How and Why We Use Information–and we are not legally required to continue to keep it.</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">For example, we keep the web server logs that record information about a visitor to one of ConvertCalculator’s websites, such as the visitor’s IP address, browser type, and operating system, for approximately 30 days. We retain the logs for this period of time in order to, among other things, analyze traffic to ConvertCalculator’s websites and investigate issues if something goes wrong on one of our websites.</p><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">Security</h2><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">While no online service is 100% secure, we work very hard to protect information about you against unauthorized access, use, alteration, or destruction, and take reasonable measures to do so, such as monitoring our Services for potential vulnerabilities and attacks.</p><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">Choices</h2><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">You have several choices available when it comes to information about you:</p><ul class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7"><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Limit the Information that You Provide:</strong>&nbsp;If you have an account with us, you can choose not to provide the optional account information, profile information, and transaction and billing information. Please keep in mind that if you do not provide this information, certain features of our Services may not be accessible.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Opt-Out of Electronic Communications:</strong>&nbsp;You may opt out of receiving promotional messages from us. Just follow the instructions in those messages. If you opt out of promotional messages, we may still send you other messages, like those about your account and legal notices.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Set Your Browser to Reject Cookies:</strong>&nbsp;At this time, ConvertCalculator does not respond to “do not track” signals across all of our Services. However, you can usually choose to set your browser to remove or reject browser cookies before using ConvertCalculator’s websites, with the drawback that certain features of ConvertCalculator’s websites may not function properly without the aid of cookies.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Close Your Account:</strong>&nbsp;While we’d be very sad to see you go, if you no longer want to use our Services :( :( :( :(, you can close your ConvertCalculator account by sending us an email at&nbsp;<!--$--><a class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ssm2ct" data-styles-preset="Nkz9BxiSz" href="mailto:info@convertcalculator.co" rel="noopener">info@convertcalculator.co</a><!--/$-->. Please keep in mind that we may continue to retain your information after closing your account, as described in How Long We Keep Information above–for example, when that information is reasonably needed to comply with (or demonstrate our compliance with) legal obligations such as law enforcement requests, or reasonably needed for our legitimate business interests.</p></li></ul><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">Your Rights</h2><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">If you are located in certain countries, including those that fall under the scope of the European General Data Protection Regulation (AKA the “GDPR”), data protection laws give you rights with respect to your personal data, subject to any exemptions provided by the law, including the rights to:</p><ul class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7"><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">Request access to your personal data;</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">Request correction or deletion of your personal data;</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">Object to our use and processing of your personal data;</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">Request that we limit our use and processing of your personal data; and</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">Request portability of your personal data.</p></li></ul><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">You can usually access, correct, or delete your personal data using your account settings and tools that we offer, but if you aren’t able to do that, or you would like to contact us about one of the other rights, scroll down to How to Reach Us to, well, find out how to reach us.</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">EU individuals also have the right to make a complaint to a government supervisory authority.</p><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">Controller</h2><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">ConvertCalculator processes information both as as Processor and as a Controller, as defined in the directive and the GDPR. ConvertCalculator will be the Controller for all information as discussed in this privacy policy. For information collected about visitors to our users’ embedded calculators, the user will be the Controller in accordance with directive and the GDPR, and ConvertCalculator will be the Processor. ConvertCalculator adheres to the directive of 1995 and the GDPR from May 25th, 2018.</p><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">How to Reach Us</h2><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">If you have a question about this Privacy Policy, or you would like to contact us about any of the rights mentioned in the Your Rights section above, please&nbsp;<!--$--><a class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ssm2ct" data-styles-preset="Nkz9BxiSz" href="../contact/">contact us</a><!--/$-->.</p><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">Other Things You Should Know <span style="--framer-text-color:var(--token-703fc757-ad09-4a5f-84d1-8f8e203a31ad, rgb(166, 162, 160))" class="framer-text">(Keep Reading!)</span></h2><h3 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-i3b3hg" data-styles-preset="Btq2R0K0E">Transferring Information</h3><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">Because ConvertCalculator’s Services are offered worldwide, the information about you that we process when you use the Services in the EU may be used, stored, and/or accessed by individuals operating outside the European Economic Area (EEA) who work for us, or third party data processors. This is required for the purposes listed in the How and Why We Use Information section above. When providing information about you to entities outside the EEA, we will take appropriate measures to ensure that the recipient protects your personal information adequately in accordance with this Privacy Policy as required by applicable law. These measures include:</p><ul class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7"><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">In the case of US based entities, entering into European Commission approved standard contractual arrangements with them, or ensuring they have signed up to the&nbsp;<!--$--><a class="framer-text" href="https://www.privacyshield.gov/welcome" rel="noopener">EU-US Privacy Shield</a><!--/$-->&nbsp;; or</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">In the case of entities based in other countries outside the EEA, entering into European Commission approved standard contractual arrangements with them.</p></li></ul><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">You can ask us for more information about the steps we take to protect your personal information when transferring it from the EU.</p><h3 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-i3b3hg" data-styles-preset="Btq2R0K0E">Visitors to Our Users' embedded calculators</h3><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">We also process information about visitors to our users’ embedded calculators on behalf of our users and in accordance with our user agreements. Please note that our processing of that information on behalf of our users for their websites isn’t covered by this Privacy Policy. We encourage our users to post a privacy policy that accurately describes their practices on data collection, use, and sharing of personal information. If you’d like, you can also read more about the data we collect on behalf of our users in our&nbsp;<!--$--><a class="framer-text" href="https://www.convertcalculator.com/privacy-notice/" rel="noopener">Privacy Notice</a><!--/$-->.</p><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">Privacy Policy Changes</h2><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">Although most changes are likely to be minor, ConvertCalculator may change its Privacy Policy from time to time. ConvertCalculator encourages visitors to frequently check this page for any changes to its Privacy Policy. If we make changes, we will notify you by revising the change log below, and, in some cases, we may provide additional notice (such as adding a statement to our website, or sending you a notification through email or your dashboard). Your further use of the Services after a change to our Privacy Policy will be subject to the updated policy.</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">That’s it! Thanks for reading.</p><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">Changelog</h2><ul class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2"                 </style><div class="framer-1t0jkii" style="transform:none" data-framer-component-type="RichTextContainer"><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">Your privacy is critically important to us. At ConvertCalculator, we have a few fundamental principles:</p><ul class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7"><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">We are thoughtful about the personal information we ask you to provide and the personal information that we collect about you through the operation of our services.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">We store personal information for only as long as we have a reason to keep it.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">We aim to make it as simple as possible for you to control what information on your website is shared publicly (or kept private), indexed by search engines, and permanently deleted.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">We help protect you from overreaching government demands for your personal information.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">We aim for full transparency on how we gather, use, and share your personal information.</p></li></ul><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">Below is our Privacy Policy, which incorporates and clarifies these principles.</p><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">Who We Are and What This Policy Covers</h2><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">Hi there! We are the guys behind ConvertCalculator.com, a embeddable web calculator that let's your create calculators (e.g. price quote calculators) to be embedded on your website.</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">This Privacy Policy applies to information that we collect about you when you use app.convertcalculator.co and when your website visitors interact with an embeddable widget.</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">Throughout this Privacy Policy we’ll refer to our website, mobile applications and other products and services collectively as “Services.”</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">Please note that this Privacy Policy does not apply to any of our products or services that have a separate privacy policy.</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">Below we explain how we collect, use, and share information about you, along with the choices that you have with respect to that information.</p><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">Information We Collect</h2><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">We only collect information about you if we have a reason to do so–for example, to provide our Services, to communicate with you, or to make our Services better.</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">We collect information in three ways: if and when you provide information to us, automatically through operating our Services, and from outside sources. Let’s go over the information that we collect.</p><h3 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-i3b3hg" data-styles-preset="Btq2R0K0E">Information You Provide to Us</h3><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">It’s probably no surprise that we collect information that you provide to us. The amount and type of information depends on the context and how we use the information. Here are some examples:</p><ul class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7"><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Basic Account Information:</strong>&nbsp;We ask for basic information from you in order to set up your account. For example, we require individuals who sign up for a app.convertcalculator.co account to provide a name, email address, password and that’s it. You may set other information like Company name, but this is not required.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Transaction and Billing Information:</strong>&nbsp;If you buy something from us, you will provide additional personal and payment information that is required to process the transaction and your payment, such as your credit card information, and contact information.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Content Information:</strong>&nbsp;Depending on the Services you use, you may also provide us with information about you. For example, if you add information about you or your company in a calculator, we will have this information, and so will anyone with access to the Internet if you choose to embed the calculator on a public page on your website.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Communications With Us (Hi There!):</strong>&nbsp;You may also provide us information when you respond to surveys, communicate with support, or any other way you contact us by posting (in the future maybe public forums).</p></li></ul><h3 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-i3b3hg" data-styles-preset="Btq2R0K0E">Information We Collect Automatically</h3><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">We also collect some information automatically:</p><ul class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7"><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Log Information:</strong>&nbsp;Like most online service providers, we collect information that web browsers, mobile devices, and servers typically make available, such as the browser type, IP address, unique device identifiers, language preference, referring site, the date and time of access, operating system, and mobile network information. We collect log information when you use our Services.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Usage Information:</strong>&nbsp;We collect information about your usage of our Services. For example, we collection event data, along with information about your device (e.g., screen size, name of cellular network, and mobile device manufacturer). We also collect information (such as referring domain) when an embedded calculator get loaded (your website visitor interacts with it). We use this information to, for example, provide our Services to you, as well as get insights on how people use our Services, so we can make our Services better.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Location Information:</strong>&nbsp;We may determine the approximate location of your device from your IP address. We collect and use this information to, for example, calculate how many people visit our Services from certain geographic regions.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Information from Cookies &amp; Other Technologies:</strong>&nbsp;A cookie is a string of information that a website stores on a visitor’s computer, and that the visitor’s browser provides to the website each time the visitor returns. Pixel tags (also called web beacons) are small blocks of code placed on websites and emails. ConvertCalculator uses cookies and other technologies like pixel tags to help us identify and track visitors, usage, and access preferences for our Services, as well as track and understand email campaign effectiveness and to deliver targeted ads. For more information about our use of cookies and other technologies for tracking, including how you can control the use of cookies, please see our Cookie Policy.</p></li></ul><h3 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-i3b3hg" data-styles-preset="Btq2R0K0E">Information We Collect from Other Sources</h3><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">We may also get information about you from other sources. For example, if you connect with a external service (such as Stripe), we will receive information from that service (such as your username, basic profile information, and friends list) via the authorization procedures used by that service. The information we receive depends on which services you authorize and any options that are available.</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">We may also get information, such as a mailing address, from third party services about individuals who are not yet our users (…but we hope will be!), which we may use, for example, for marketing and advertising purposes like postcards and other mailers advertising our services.</p><h3 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-i3b3hg" data-styles-preset="Btq2R0K0E">Information we collect from the Google Sheets integration</h3><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">When authorizing us to use your Google user data, we collect spreadsheet properties when you integrate a calculator with Google Sheets. We access a list of your Google Drive files in order for you to pick a spreadsheet. When you selected a spreadsheet, we access the spreadsheet's properties to present you the option to choose the preferred worksheet. After that, we read the first row's values in order for you to connect calculator form fields to spreadsheet columns. When a submission is made on your calculator, we append the calculator form field values to the selected spreadsheet. In terms of storage, we only save the Spreadsheet ID and the sheet ID (also called Worksheet ID). We don't share any Google user data.</p><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">How And Why We Use Information</h2><h3 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-i3b3hg" data-styles-preset="Btq2R0K0E">Purposes for Using Information</h3><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">We use information about you as mentioned above and for the purposes listed below:</p><ul class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7"><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">To provide our Services–for example, to set up and maintain your account, host your embed code, or charge you for any of our paid Services;</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">To further develop and improve our Services–for example by adding new features that we think our users will enjoy or will help them to create and manage their websites more efficiently;</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">To monitor and analyze trends and better understand how users interact with our Services, which helps us improve our Services and make them easier to use;</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">To measure, gauge, and improve the effectiveness of our advertising, and better understand user retention and attrition–for example, we may analyze how many individuals purchased a plan after receiving a marketing message or the features used by those who continue to use our Services after a certain length of time;</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">To monitor and prevent any problems with our Services, protect the security of our Services, detect and prevent fraudulent transactions and other illegal activities, fight spam, and protect the rights and property of ConvertCalculator and others, which may result in us declining a transaction or the use of our Services;</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">To communicate with you, for example through an email, about offers and promotions offered by ConvertCalculator and others we think will be of interest to you, solicit your feedback, or keep you up to date on ConvertCalculator and our products; and</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">To personalize your experience using our Services, target our marketing messages to groups of our users (for example, those who have a particular plan with us or have been our user for a certain length of time), and serve relevant advertisements.</p></li></ul><h3 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-i3b3hg" data-styles-preset="Btq2R0K0E">Legal Bases for Collecting and Using Information</h3><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">A note here for those in the European Union about our legal grounds for processing information about you under EU data protection laws, which is that our use of your information is based on the grounds that:</p><ol class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7"><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">The use is necessary in order to fulfill our commitments to you under our Terms of Service or other agreements with you or is necessary to administer your account–for example, in order to enable access to our website on your device or charge you for a paid plan; or</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">The use is necessary for compliance with a legal obligation; or</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">The use is necessary in order to protect your vital interests or those of another person; or</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">We have a legitimate interest in using your information–for example, to provide and update our Services, to improve our Services so that we can offer you an even better user experience, to safeguard our Services, to communicate with you, to measure, gauge, and improve the effectiveness of our advertising, and better understand user retention and attrition, to monitor and prevent any problems with our Services, and to personalize your experience; or</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">You have given us your consent–for example when you create your account.</p></li></ol><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">Sharing Information</h2><h3 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-i3b3hg" data-styles-preset="Btq2R0K0E">How We Share Information</h3><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">We do not sell our users’ private personal information.</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">We share information about you in the limited circumstances spelled out below and with appropriate safeguards on your privacy:</p><ul class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7"><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Subsidiaries, Employees, and Independent Contractors:</strong>&nbsp;We may disclose information about you to our subsidiaries, our employees, and individuals who are our independent contractors that need to know the information in order to help us provide our Services or to process the information on our behalf. We require our subsidiaries, employees, and independent contractors to follow this Privacy Policy for personal information that we share with them.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Third Party Vendors:</strong>&nbsp;We may share information about you with third party vendors who need to know information about you in order to provide their services to us, or to provide their services to you or your site. This group includes vendors that help us provide our Services to you (like payment providers that process your credit and debit card information, fraud prevention services that allow us to analyze fraudulent payment transactions, postal and email delivery services that help us stay in touch with you, customer chat and email support services that help us communicate with you, those that assist us with our marketing efforts (e.g. by providing tools for identifying a specific marketing target group or improving our marketing campaigns), those that help us understand and enhance our Services (like analytics providers). We require vendors to agree to privacy commitments in order to share information with them.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Legal Requests:</strong>&nbsp;We may disclose information about you in response to a subpoena, court order, or other governmental request.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">To Protect Rights, Property, and Others:</strong>&nbsp;We may disclose information about you when we believe in good faith that disclosure is reasonably necessary to protect the property or rights of ConvertCalculator, third parties, or the public at large. For example, if we have a good faith belief that there is an imminent danger of death or serious physical injury, we may disclose information related to the emergency without delay.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Business Transfers:</strong>&nbsp;In connection with any merger, sale of company assets, or acquisition of all or a portion of our business by another company, or in the unlikely event that ConvertCalculator goes out of business or enters bankruptcy, user information would likely be one of the assets that is transferred or acquired by a third party. If any of these events were to happen, this Privacy Policy would continue to apply to your information and the party receiving your information may continue to use your information, but only consistent with this Privacy Policy.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">With Your Consent:</strong>&nbsp;We may share and disclose information with your consent or at your direction. For example, we may share your information with third parties with which you authorize us to do so, such as the social media services that you connect to your site through our Publicize feature.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Aggregated or De-Identified Information:</strong>&nbsp;We may share information that has been aggregated or reasonably de-identified, so that the information could not reasonably be used to identify you. For instance, we may publish aggregate statistics about the use of our Services and we may share a hashed version of your email address to facilitate customized ad campaigns on other platforms.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Published Support Requests:</strong>&nbsp;And if you send us a request (for example, via a support email or one of our feedback mechanisms), we reserve the right to publish that request in order to help us clarify or respond to your request or to help us support other users.</p></li></ul><h3 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-i3b3hg" data-styles-preset="Btq2R0K0E">Information Shared Publicly</h3><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">Information that you choose to make public is–you guessed it–disclosed publicly.</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">That means, of course, that all information you put in a calculator that you embed on your website, are all available to others–and we hope you get a lot of visitors!</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">Public information may also be indexed by search engines or used by third parties.</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">Please keep all of this in mind when deciding what you would like to share.</p><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">How Long We Keep Information</h2><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">We generally discard information about you when we no longer need the information for the purposes for which we collect and use it–which are described in the section above on How and Why We Use Information–and we are not legally required to continue to keep it.</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">For example, we keep the web server logs that record information about a visitor to one of ConvertCalculator’s websites, such as the visitor’s IP address, browser type, and operating system, for approximately 30 days. We retain the logs for this period of time in order to, among other things, analyze traffic to ConvertCalculator’s websites and investigate issues if something goes wrong on one of our websites.</p><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">Security</h2><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">While no online service is 100% secure, we work very hard to protect information about you against unauthorized access, use, alteration, or destruction, and take reasonable measures to do so, such as monitoring our Services for potential vulnerabilities and attacks.</p><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">Choices</h2><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">You have several choices available when it comes to information about you:</p><ul class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7"><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Limit the Information that You Provide:</strong>&nbsp;If you have an account with us, you can choose not to provide the optional account information, profile information, and transaction and billing information. Please keep in mind that if you do not provide this information, certain features of our Services may not be accessible.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Opt-Out of Electronic Communications:</strong>&nbsp;You may opt out of receiving promotional messages from us. Just follow the instructions in those messages. If you opt out of promotional messages, we may still send you other messages, like those about your account and legal notices.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Set Your Browser to Reject Cookies:</strong>&nbsp;At this time, ConvertCalculator does not respond to “do not track” signals across all of our Services. However, you can usually choose to set your browser to remove or reject browser cookies before using ConvertCalculator’s websites, with the drawback that certain features of ConvertCalculator’s websites may not function properly without the aid of cookies.</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text"><strong class="framer-text">Close Your Account:</strong>&nbsp;While we’d be very sad to see you go, if you no longer want to use our Services :( :( :( :(, you can close your ConvertCalculator account by sending us an email at&nbsp;<!--$--><a class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ssm2ct" data-styles-preset="Nkz9BxiSz" href="mailto:info@convertcalculator.co" rel="noopener">info@convertcalculator.co</a><!--/$-->. Please keep in mind that we may continue to retain your information after closing your account, as described in How Long We Keep Information above–for example, when that information is reasonably needed to comply with (or demonstrate our compliance with) legal obligations such as law enforcement requests, or reasonably needed for our legitimate business interests.</p></li></ul><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">Your Rights</h2><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">If you are located in certain countries, including those that fall under the scope of the European General Data Protection Regulation (AKA the “GDPR”), data protection laws give you rights with respect to your personal data, subject to any exemptions provided by the law, including the rights to:</p><ul class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7"><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">Request access to your personal data;</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">Request correction or deletion of your personal data;</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">Object to our use and processing of your personal data;</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">Request that we limit our use and processing of your personal data; and</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">Request portability of your personal data.</p></li></ul><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">You can usually access, correct, or delete your personal data using your account settings and tools that we offer, but if you aren’t able to do that, or you would like to contact us about one of the other rights, scroll down to How to Reach Us to, well, find out how to reach us.</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">EU individuals also have the right to make a complaint to a government supervisory authority.</p><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">Controller</h2><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">ConvertCalculator processes information both as as Processor and as a Controller, as defined in the directive and the GDPR. ConvertCalculator will be the Controller for all information as discussed in this privacy policy. For information collected about visitors to our users’ embedded calculators, the user will be the Controller in accordance with directive and the GDPR, and ConvertCalculator will be the Processor. ConvertCalculator adheres to the directive of 1995 and the GDPR from May 25th, 2018.</p><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">How to Reach Us</h2><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">If you have a question about this Privacy Policy, or you would like to contact us about any of the rights mentioned in the Your Rights section above, please&nbsp;<!--$--><a class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ssm2ct" data-styles-preset="Nkz9BxiSz" href="../contact/">contact us</a><!--/$-->.</p><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">Other Things You Should Know <span style="--framer-text-color:var(--token-703fc757-ad09-4a5f-84d1-8f8e203a31ad, rgb(166, 162, 160))" class="framer-text">(Keep Reading!)</span></h2><h3 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-i3b3hg" data-styles-preset="Btq2R0K0E">Transferring Information</h3><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">Because ConvertCalculator’s Services are offered worldwide, the information about you that we process when you use the Services in the EU may be used, stored, and/or accessed by individuals operating outside the European Economic Area (EEA) who work for us, or third party data processors. This is required for the purposes listed in the How and Why We Use Information section above. When providing information about you to entities outside the EEA, we will take appropriate measures to ensure that the recipient protects your personal information adequately in accordance with this Privacy Policy as required by applicable law. These measures include:</p><ul class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7"><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">In the case of US based entities, entering into European Commission approved standard contractual arrangements with them, or ensuring they have signed up to the&nbsp;<!--$--><a class="framer-text" href="https://www.privacyshield.gov/welcome" rel="noopener">EU-US Privacy Shield</a><!--/$-->&nbsp;; or</p></li><li class="framer-text"><p class="framer-text">In the case of entities based in other countries outside the EEA, entering into European Commission approved standard contractual arrangements with them.</p></li></ul><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">You can ask us for more information about the steps we take to protect your personal information when transferring it from the EU.</p><h3 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-i3b3hg" data-styles-preset="Btq2R0K0E">Visitors to Our Users' embedded calculators</h3><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">We also process information about visitors to our users’ embedded calculators on behalf of our users and in accordance with our user agreements. Please note that our processing of that information on behalf of our users for their websites isn’t covered by this Privacy Policy. We encourage our users to post a privacy policy that accurately describes their practices on data collection, use, and sharing of personal information. If you’d like, you can also read more about the data we collect on behalf of our users in our&nbsp;<!--$--><a class="framer-text" href="https://www.convertcalculator.com/privacy-notice/" rel="noopener">Privacy Notice</a><!--/$-->.</p><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">Privacy Policy Changes</h2><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">Although most changes are likely to be minor, ConvertCalculator may change its Privacy Policy from time to time. ConvertCalculator encourages visitors to frequently check this page for any changes to its Privacy Policy. If we make changes, we will notify you by revising the change log below, and, in some cases, we may provide additional notice (such as adding a statement to our website, or sending you a notification through email or your dashboard). Your further use of the Services after a change to our Privacy Policy will be subject to the updated policy.</p><p class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2" data-styles-preset="PPy8h4aL7">That’s it! Thanks for reading.</p><h2 class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-t82kk1" data-styles-preset="VcPcSqxdo">Changelog</h2><ul class="framer-text framer-styles-preset-ff9rp2"               <h2>1. What is this Privacy Policy?</h2>
    <p>We appreciate your trust and work hard to properly protect your personal data. We respect your privacy and undertake to lawfully process and protect your personal data in accordance with all legal requirements, including those of the EU General Data Protection Regulation 2016/679 (<strong>“GDPR”</strong>).</p>
    <p>In this privacy policy (<strong>“Privacy Policy”</strong>) we will provide you with information about the ways that MB “Lumius” (<strong>“the Company”</strong>) processes your personal data obtained in the process of: providing services to you; direct marketing activities; implementing agreements between the Company and counter parties / legal persons; promoting the Company’s publicity; you visiting the Company’s website or social media sites; you sending inquiries. All persons mentioned hereinafter shall be referred to as <strong>data subjects</strong>.  </p>
    <h2>2. About the Company</h2>
    <p>The Company is MB “Lumius”, company reg. no. 304227411, office address: A. Goštauto str. 8-136, Vilnius, the Republic of Lithuania. If you have any questions related to personal data protection, contact us at dpo@lumifish.com. </p>
    <h2>3. What are personal data?</h2>
    <p>Personal data include any information about a data subject collected by the Company that can be used to identify such data subject and are protected electronically or otherwise.</p>
    <p>Personal data includes any information such as the first name / surname and email address of a data subject collected by the Company for the purposes specified in this Privacy Policy or a separate data subject consent form or agreement concluded with the Company.</p>
    <h2>4. Personal data processed in the process of providing the services of the Company</h2>
    <p>We must process your personal data to provide you with high-quality services, process your payments for services provided, etc. </p>
    <p>We might need to process your first name, surname, email address and residential address for the purposes of service provision. We may also process information about a service plan chosen by you, your payments and the date on which we started providing you with our services.</p>
    <p>To process your payments for provided services, we might need to process information about the type of your payment card and the last four digits of the card number. When you use PayPal to pay for our services, we may also process your PayPal ID.  </p>
    <p>All personal data shall be processed to fulfill our contractual obligations towards you (Art. 6(1)b (Contract) GDPR). </p>
    <p>All personal data shall be obtained only from you and disclosed only to service providers chosen by the Company for the purposes of providing you with services or fulfilling legal requirements.</p>
    <p>Your personal data shall be processed for the duration of the provision of services and for another 10 years after the end of the provision of services.</p>
    <p>If you refuse to provide your personal data, the Company will not be able to provide you with services.</p>
    <h2>5. Direct marketing</h2>
    <p>Persons who provided their email address and expressed their willingness to receive information about the services of the Company, its products, newsletters and other promotional material might receive the Company's emails with proposals of our services, newsletters or other promotional material.</p>
    <p>The Company will process your email address for the purposes of direct marketing. For the purposes of direct marketing, your data will be processed for 3 years from the time of you providing consent. </p>
    <p>You have the right to opt out of direct marketing correspondence by emailing us at the address provided herein or the canceling newsletter subscription. This shall not impose any negative consequences for you.</p>
